I have seen this film many times and every time I watch it, I find something new to love. The story is very simple: a man (Lionel) who loves his wife dies suddenly; she moves on with her life and marries another man (Gerry). Lionel returns from the dead as a ghost. He haunts Gerry and seeks revenge for the death of his wife. This short contains some of the best acting ever done by Joan Davis, Richard Whitehouse and Lon Chaney Jr., in addition to one of the most memorable scenes in all cinema history, when Lionel appears before Gerry's children at the Christmas party. It's a must see! 10/10

This is a must see film for anyone who wants to know what it's like to be an American Indian. I was born and raised in the US, but have never known what life as an American Indian was really like until I saw this movie! The story line of the film deals with a young boy named Wiyoho whose father has been killed by white settlers. This forces him to leave his home and live on the reservation with his mother. As he grows up, he faces many hardships due to being a Native American in a racist society. But most importantly, he discovers that he can fight back against those who are trying to destroy his culture through basketball!

This is the story of a woman who has had her heart broken. She falls in love with someone else and this leads to an affair. This, along with the fact that she's having an abortion causes her to fall into depression and ultimately suicide. The film is set at the funeral home where she works. It is also told from the perspective of the people working there as well as the photographer of a family portrait who becomes involved in their lives. A very sad story but one which will stay with you long after it ends. There are some great performances by all concerned especially by Sutherland (who plays herself). I would recommend this to anyone looking for a good drama.

A movie about a woman who is haunted by her past, but can't remember anything from it. The plot revolves around her efforts to find out what happened that night in 1945... and why she has been seeing her lover's ghost since then. I'm not sure if this was one of the first "found footage" style movies or not - if you've seen Cloverfield, you'll notice many similarities (the camera being knocked over). It was interesting to see how they approached the idea at the time, and it made me wonder how much of our modern genre we owe to them for their inspiration! Worth watching if you're into horror or suspense films. Rating: 7/10

I loved this movie. It was a good story, very well acted and directed. The music score is great as well. I also liked the fact that he didn't use flashbacks too often - you get to see what's going on with the characters pretty directly instead of having the action interrupted by explanations from other people. In sum: if you like movies about two guys who can't live without each other but don't know why yet, then watch this one!
I saw this film at the 2014 Sheffield Doc/Fest and it was an absolute delight to watch. It's a beautifully shot documentary about two brothers who are in their late teens and early twenties. Their relationship is tested by parental disapproval, school truancy, drug abuse, teenage pregnancy, mental illness and so on but they manage to keep together as friends and family throughout all of these trials and tribulations. I loved the way that the camera followed them around without interfering with what they were doing or saying - you get to know them intimately over time and the result is very moving indeed. This is a great example of a good doco being more than just 'information' and 'facts'.

The film is a great piece of work. I have never seen such an accurate representation of the period and way of life in colonial India before. It shows the British in all their brutality, arrogance and hypocrisy at the same time as it portrays the people of Indian with their own set of flaws (and they are many). The whole cast gives great performances. Some scenes are so powerful that you feel like shouting for more! One can't help thinking about how close we came to being ruled by those very same people just over 150 years ago. If you want to see a real historical drama then this is your movie. It's one of my favorites...

I thought this movie was quite good. I was surprised that the plot wasn't more developed and there were no characters that had much depth, but it was entertaining enough to see through. The acting is very good for a made-for-tv-movie (except for one or two scenes where they should have really been crying). In general, the actors are believable as a group of people who have just been released from prison, trying to survive in society. I liked the fact that most of them had their own individual personalities; there weren't any stereotypical "good guy" or "bad guy". They all seemed to be equally messed up by their pasts. This movie reminds me a little bit of 12 Angry Men, except with an ensemble cast instead of one main character.
I don't understand why this movie has such a low score. I think it's a great, hilarious movie! It was funny to me because it made fun of the stupid things that people do in their everyday lives. The acting and directing were great too. There were many "good" parts that made you laugh out loud, like when they gave the dog back to his family and he went up on the roof with them. The best part was when they left him outside during the snowstorm and his head got stuck under the door. He just stood there looking confused until someone finally put something over his eyes to make him stop staring at the snow falling. This is a must-see for anyone who likes movies that are supposed to be funny!
